[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow was detected during fuzz testing of the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer`. The overflow occurs in the function [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data_entry` within `libexif/exif-data.c` when reading and copying [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata from a provided input buffer. The fuzzer triggers a [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-byte read [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately past the end of a [0m[1;36m207[0m[39m-byte allocation, leading to an out-of-bounds [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory access.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue: While running the fuzzer `exif_from_data_fuzzer` in interactive mode with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLibFuzzer, a heap-buffer-overflow is reported. The fuzzer invokes [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_new_from_data`, which calls into `exif_data_load_data`, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data_content`, and then `exif_data_load_data_entry`. During a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcpy` in `exif_data_load_data_entry`, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes are read from an address that is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly one byte past the end of a [0m[1;36m207[0m[39m-byte allocated region.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type: heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmulti-byte read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is flagged at `__asan_memcpy` when copying data in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:213[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The offending read is size [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, from address `[0m[1;36m0x51100000024f[0m[39m`, which is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after the allocated block `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x511000000180[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x51100000024f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Allocation of the buffer occurs via `operator new` during the fuzzer’s input [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling, without subsequent resizing before the copy.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Stack trace highlights the chain:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput → calls `exif_data_new_from_data`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `exif_data_load_data` → `exif_data_load_data_content` → [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data_entry`  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `memcpy` invoked on a buffer that is too small.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Investigation:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • exif-data.c around lines [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m213[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m531[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m984[0m[39m: review how buffer lengths and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent lengths are determined and validated before `memcpy`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Data structures and length fields used to describe EXIF tags and data entries. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEnsure that any length values supplied by external inputs are checked against [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual buffer sizes.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sequence of function calls in `exif_data_load_data*` family to identify [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere bounds checking is missing or incorrect.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc` at line [0m[1;36m51[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows how raw input [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis passed into the library; while not the root cause, it indicates which API [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurfaces are exercised.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue demonstrates a direct out-of-bounds read in the core EXIF parsing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines and warrants a thorough audit of all memory-copy operations in `libexif`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticularly those handling lengths derived from external data.[0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m234[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m235[0m[39m:    [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m236[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:425[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m443[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m425[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Read the number of entries *[0m[35m/[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m426[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset, ds, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m427[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m428[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"Tag data past end of buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u+2 > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, offset, ds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m429[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m430[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m431[0m[39m:    [0m[39mn = exif_get_short [0m[1;39m([0m[39md + offset, data->priv->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m432[0m[39m:    [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m433[0m[39m:    [0m[39m          [0m[32m"Loading %hu entries..."[0m[39m, n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m434[0m[39m:    [0m[39moffset += [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m435[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m436[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Check if we have enough data. *[0m[35m/[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m437[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset, ds, [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m*n[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m438[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mn = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mds - offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m439[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m440[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"Short data; only loading %hu entries..."[0m[39m, n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m441[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m442[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m443[0m[39m:    [0m[39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < n; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:931[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m940[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m931[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m932[0m[39m:    [0m[39m * Verify the exif header[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m933[0m[39m:    [0m[39m * [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, length [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m934[0m[39m:    [0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m935[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mds < [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m936[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mLOG_TOO_SMALL;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m937[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m938[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m939[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemcmp [0m[1;39m([0m[39md, ExifHeader, [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m940[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:975[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m983[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m975[0m[39m:    [0m[39moffset = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39md + [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, data->priv->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m976[0m[39m:    [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m977[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"IFD 0 at %i."[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m978[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m979[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* ds is restricted to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bit above, so offset is restricted too, and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset+[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m should not overflow. *[0m[35m/[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m980[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset > ds || offset + [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m > ds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m981[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m982[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m983[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Parse the actual exif data [0m[1;39m([0m[39musually offset [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m from start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐cause analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In exif_data_load_data_entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif-data.[0m[1;92mc:159[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m236[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the bounds checks use the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal “size” parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe length of the current IFD‐entry slice[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull length of the internal EXIF data buffer.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During parsing, load_data and load_data_content slice the raw buffer for IFD [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtables but do not reduce the “size” parameter passed to load_data_entry properly. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAs a result, “size” can exceed the real allocation length of the raw data buffer, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing doff + s reads beyond the heap allocation.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ASan report shows a [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m‐byte memcpy at an address one byte past the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m207[0m[39m‐byte buffer: doff was computed from untrusted input, “size” was too large, so [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m …; if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m …;` passed, and memcpy read [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout of bounds.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve critical logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must still enforce [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m numeric overflows in s = format_size × components, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m zero‐ or negative‐size checks, and [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m slice‐level sanity logging for corrupt [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor truncated IFD tables.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter the public API, fuzzer harness, or test code. We only modify[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal library routines in exif-data.c.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy to fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Leverage the ExifDataPrivate raw‐buffer size field [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe true allocation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength of data->priv->data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In exif_data_new_from_data, the raw input is copied into data->priv->data [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand its length stored in data->priv->size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor a similarly named field[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We will [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm this with a brief code lookup.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. In exif_data_load_data_entry, change the bounds checks to compare against [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata->priv->size instead of the local “size” parameter when deciding whether it is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe to memcpy from `d + doff`:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Retain the local “size” checks for determining slice validity and logging,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut do not let them implicitly authorize reading beyond the real buffer.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Add or replace:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= data->priv->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag starts past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u >= %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata->priv->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > data->priv->size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoff + s, data->priv->size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Only after these checks perform `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry->data, d + doff, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Rationale: by validating against the actual allocated buffer length, we close[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe gap introduced by the slice‐length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“size”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m being out of sync with the real [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer. This prevents any doff + s read from exceeding the heap allocation.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open libexif/exif-data.c and locate exif_data_load_data_entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m159[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. After computing `doff` and `s` and before the existing `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck, insert:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int full_size = data->priv->size;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= full_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[32m"Tag starts past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u >= %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > full_size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff + s, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Optionally retain or remove the slice‐based `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey become redundant once full_size checks are in place[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun the fuzzer to verify the ASan heap-buffer-overflow no [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger triggers.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Run existing unit tests to ensure no regressions.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and side‐effects[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves the IFD parsing and logging logic, only tightening [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds against the real buffer.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not alter any public symbols or the fuzzer harness, so existing tests [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand fuzz targets remain valid.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By using data->priv->size, we ensure any EXIF entries referring to data [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manywhere in the buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39meven beyond the IFD section[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are safely checked against the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue allocation, avoiding both under‐ and over‐reporting of corrupt data.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The added checks are strictly more conservative; they will only reject entries[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat truly reference outside the original EXIF data. Any valid entries entirely [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the buffer will still load.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Confirm private‐size field[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that ExifDataPrivate indeed has a length field, e.g. `unsigned int [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize;` or `data_len`, by inspecting the struct near the top of exif-data.c or its [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the field uses a different name, adjust the patch accordingly [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`data->priv->data_length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Final step[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Commit the patch to exif-data.c with a clear description: “Fix [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in exif_data_load_data_entry by replacing slice‐length checks [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith full‐buffer‐length checks.”  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer `exif_from_data_fuzzer` triggered an AddressSanitizer [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in libexif’s `exif_data_load_data_entry` function when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a malformed EXIF block. The issue manifests as a multi-byte read just [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpast the end of an allocated heap buffer. A patch was attempted to add extra sanity[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks against a presumed full-buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`data->priv->size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in addition to the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting slice-size checks, but the build failed because `ExifDataPrivate` does not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontain a `size` member. The compilation error halted further progress.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzing run of `exif_from_data_fuzzer` on `libexif` produced:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ==[0m[1;36m18[0m[39m==ERROR: AddressSanitizer: heap-buffer-overflow on address [0m[1;36m0x51100000024f[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  READ of size [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m at [0m[1;36m0x51100000024f[0m[39m thread T0[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0x55f9199bcff1[0m[39m in __asan_memcpy[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0x55f919a03219[0m[39m in exif_data_load_data_entry [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m213[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m … in exif_data_load_data_content [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m531[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m … in exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m984[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m … in exif_data_new_from_data [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-data.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m159[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  #[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m … in LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput [0m[1;39m([0m[35m/src/[0m[95mexif_from_data_fuzzer.cc[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m51[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow occurred because the code uses `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry->data, d + doff, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter only checking against a local slice length `size`, not against the full [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer length held by the `ExifData` structure.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocated region was exactly [0m[1;36m207[0m[39m bytes long, and the code attempted to read [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m bytes starting at offset [0m[1;36m207[0m[39m, resulting in reading one byte past the allocation.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic function is `exif_data_load_data_entry` in `libexif/exif-data.c`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parameters `d` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpointer to entry data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `size` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength of this slice[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m come[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom a higher‐level read of the EXIF blob.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A field `data->priv->order` determines endianness, and `exif_get_long` reads an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset from the data slice.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After computing `doff`, existing code checks only that `doff < size` and `s <= [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize - doff` before doing a `memcpy`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch added an extra set of bounds checks against a presumed “full buffer size”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39musing `data->priv->size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before preserving the original slice-based checks. The [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiff applied to `libexif/exif-data.c` around line [0m[1;36m189[0m[39m in function [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data_entry` was:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```diff[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m--- a/libexif/exif-data.c[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+++ b/libexif/exif-data.c[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m@@ [0m[1;36m-189[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m23[0m[39m +[0m[1;36m189[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m38[0m[39m @@[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mdoff = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39md + offset + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, data->priv->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39melse[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mdoff = offset + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Sanity checks *[0m[35m/[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Check against full buffer size *[0m[35m/[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= full_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag starts past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u >= %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff, [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff + s, [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying this change, the build error was:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif-data.[0m[1;92mc:199:46[0m[39m: error: no member named [0m[32m'size'[0m[39m in [0m[32m'struct _ExifDataPrivate'[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  unsigned int full_size = data->priv->size;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                        ^~~~[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis indicates that the field `size` does not exist in `ExifDataPrivate`, so the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch cannot access the intended buffer-length value.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Further Investigation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully understand and resolve the overflow, the following areas should be [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexamined:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Definition of `ExifDataPrivate`**  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect `libexif/exif-data.h` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor related private headers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to identify how the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull EXIF data buffer length is stored and accessed.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Determine if there is a differently named field [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `data->priv->blob_size`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor a separate cursor/length member[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Callers of `exif_data_load_data_entry`**  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Trace how `d` and `size` are derived in `exif_data_load_data_content` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that these callers correctly pass the slice pointer/length and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand their relationship to the overall buffer.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer Ownership and Lifetime**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm how memory is allocated for the EXIF blob [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., via [0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The sanitizer report shows that exif_data_load_data_entry only checks tag [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`doff`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`s`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m against the IFD slice size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not against[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe true EXIF payload buffer. Upstream code in exif_data_load_data captures the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull APP1 section length in a local variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fullds`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but never stores it. [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mConsequently, exif_data_load_data_entry cannot perform robust bounds checks and may[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread past the heap buffer. The previous patch failed because it referenced a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-existent `data->priv->size` member.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Introduce a `full_size` Member  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify the private data structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39min exif-data.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to record the actual slice [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength seen by the loader:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     struct _ExifDataPrivate [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifByteOrder    order;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifMnoteData   *md;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifLog         *log;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifMem         *mem;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int     ref_count;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Temporarily used while loading data *[0m[35m/[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int     offset_mnote;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Actual EXIF payload length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mslice after header[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, for bounds checks *[0m[35m/[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        unsigned int     full_size;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifDataOption   options;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ExifDataType     data_type;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Because the private structure is zero-initialized [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia the existing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `full_size` defaults to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, ensuring no unexpected behavior on code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths that never set it.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Record the [0m[3;92mTrue[0m[39m Buffer Length in `exif_data_load_data`  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter locating the APP1 marker, capping the section to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0xFFFE[0m[39m, and subtracting the [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m-byte header[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, store the resulting slice length into [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`data->priv->full_size`. For example:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* After: fullds = original ds; if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mds > [0m[1;36m0xfffe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ds = [0m[1;36m0xfffe[0m[39m; *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ds -= [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m skip the [0m[32m"Exif\0\0"[0m[39m header[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d  += [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     data->priv->full_size = ds;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that downstream entry loaders know the full valid range for tag [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Strengthen Bounds Checks in `exif_data_load_data_entry`  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In exif_data_load_data_entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore the existing slice bounds checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsert:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Sanity checks against the full EXIF payload *[0m[35m/[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= data->priv->full_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Tag starts past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u >= %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  doff, data->priv->full_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > data->priv->full_size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of full buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  doff + s, data->priv->full_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the existing slice checks against the local `size` parameter to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserve backward compatibility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey protect against cases where the IFD slice is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msmaller than the overall payload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing checks and downstream processing remain untouched.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new `full_size` checks only reject malformed tags that would read beyond [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe heap buffer.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing logic, public API, or utility functions are modified. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExisting tests and thumbnail functionality remain unaffected.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `libexif/exif-data.c`, locate the `_ExifDataPrivate` struct [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and insert the `full_size` member.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `exif_data_load_data` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m950[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m956[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, after subtracting the [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m-byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ds -= [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m; d += [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add `data->priv->full_size = ds;`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In `exif_data_load_data_entry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m190[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before the existing slice [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks, insert the two full-buffer sanity checks referencing [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`data->priv->full_size`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Recompile and run the fuzzer to confirm the overflow is eliminated without [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Analysis  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By storing the true payload length, we ensure all tag reads are bounded by the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual heap buffer, eliminating the overflow.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The additional `full_size` checks trigger early returns only on malformed EXIF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata; valid images are unaffected.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any code path that does not call `exif_data_load_data` will see `full_size == [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m` and fail safe [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtags are skipped[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preventing unsafe reads.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach parallels existing slice-and-full-buffer checks in other [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimage-parsing libraries, ensuring robust fuzz-safe behavior.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo external dependencies or harness modifications are required. Apply all changes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min a single patch to the initial codebase to resolve the issue.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
